err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\treturn o.Validate()\n}\n\n// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\nfunc (o *OAuth2) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n\tif o == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\to.ClientSecretFile = JoinDir(dir, o.ClientSecretFile)\n\to.TLSConfig.SetDirectory(dir)\n}\n\n// LoadHTTPConfig parses the YAML input s into a HTTPClientConfig.\nfunc LoadHTTPConfig(s string) (*HTTPClientConfig, error) {\n\tcfg := &HTTPClientConfig{}\n\terr := yaml.UnmarshalStrict([]byte(s), cfg)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\treturn cfg, nil\n}\n\n// LoadHTTPConfigFile parses the given YAML file into a HTTPClientConfig.\nfunc LoadHTTPConfigFile(filename string) (*HTTPClientConfig, []byte, error) {\n\tcontent, err := os.ReadFile(filename)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n\t}\n\tcfg, err := LoadHTTPConfig(string(content))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n\t}\n\tcfg.SetDirectory(filepath.Dir(filepath.Dir(filename)))\n\treturn cfg, content, nil\n}\n\n// HTTPClientConfig configures an HTTP client.\ntype HTTPClientConfig struct {\n\t// The HTTP basic authentication credentials for the targets.\n\tBasicAuth *BasicAuth `yaml:\"basic_auth,omitempty\" json:\"basic_auth,omitempty\"`\n\t// The HTTP authorization credentials for the targets.\n\tAuthorization *Authorization `yaml:\"authorization,omitempty\" json:\"authorization,omitempty\"`\n\t// The OAuth2 client credentials used to fetch a token for the targets.\n\tOAuth2 *OAuth2 `yaml:\"oauth2,omitempty\" json:\"oauth2,omitempty\"`\n\t// The bearer token for the targets. Deprecated in favour of\n\t// Authorization.Credentials.\n\tBearerToken Secret `yaml:\"bearer_token,omitempty\" json:\"bearer_token,omitempty\"`\n\t// The bearer token file for the targets. Deprecated in favour of\n\t// Authorization.CredentialsFile.\n\tBearerTokenFile string `yaml:\"bearer_token_file,omitempty\" json:\"bearer_token_file,omitempty\"`\n\t// TLSConfig to use to connect to the targets.\n\tTLSConfig TLSConfig `yaml:\"tls_config,omitempty\" json:\"tls_config,omitempty\"`\n\t// FollowRedirects specifies whether the client should follow HTTP 3xx redirects.\n\t// The omitempty flag is not set, because it would be hidden from the\n\t// marshalled configuration when set to false.\n\tFollowRedirects bool `yaml:\"follow_redirects\" json:\"follow_redirects\"`\n\t// EnableHTTP2 specifies whether the client should configure HTTP2.\n\t// The omitempty flag is not set, because it would be hidden from the\n\t// marshalled configuration when set to false.\n\tEnableHTTP2 bool `yaml:\"enable_http2\" json:\"enable_http2\"`\n\t// Proxy configuration.\n\tProxyConfig `yaml:\",inline\"`\n\t// HTTPHeaders specify headers to inject in the requests. Those headers\n\t// could be marshalled back to the users.\n\tHTTPHeaders *Headers `yaml:\"http_headers,omitempty\" json:\"http_headers,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\nfunc (c *HTTPClientConfig) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n\tif c == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tc.TLSConfig.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tc.BasicAuth.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tc.Authorization.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tc.OAuth2.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tc.HTTPHeaders.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tc.BearerTokenFile = JoinDir(dir, c.BearerTokenFile)\n}\n\n// nonZeroCount returns the amount of values that are non-zero.\nfunc nonZeroCount[T comparable](values ...T) int {\n\tcount := 0\n\tvar zero T\n\tfor _, value := range values {\n\t\tif value != zero {\n\t\t\tcount++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn count\n}\n\n// Validate validates the HTTPClientConfig to check only one of BearerToken,\n// BasicAuth and BearerTokenFile is configured. It also validates that ProxyURL\n// is set if ProxyConnectHeader is set.\nfunc (c *HTTPClientConfig) Validate() error {\n\t// Backwards compatibility with the bearer_token field.\n\tif len(c.BearerToken) > 0 && len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of bearer_token & bearer_token_file must be configured\")\n\t}\n\tif (c.BasicAuth != nil || c.OAuth2 != nil) && (len(c.BearerToken) > 0 || len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0) {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth, oauth2, bearer_token & bearer_token_file must be configured\")\n\t}\n\tif c.BasicAuth != nil && nonZeroCount(c.BasicAuth.Username != \"\", c.BasicAuth.UsernameFile != \"\", c.BasicAuth.UsernameRef != \"\") > 1 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth username, username_file & username_ref must be configured\")\n\t}\n\tif c.BasicAuth != nil && nonZeroCount(string(c.BasicAuth.Password) != \"\", c.BasicAuth.PasswordFile != \"\", c.BasicAuth.PasswordRef != \"\") > 1 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth password, password_file & password_ref must be configured\")\n\t}\n\tif c.Authorization != nil {\n\t\tif len(c.BearerToken) > 0 || len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"authorization is not compatible with bearer_token & bearer_token_file\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tif nonZeroCount(string(c.Authorization.Credentials) != \"\", c.Authorization.CredentialsFile != \"\", c.Authorization.CredentialsRef != \"\") > 1 {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of authorization credentials & credentials_file must be configured\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tc.Authorization.Type = strings.TrimSpace(c.Authorization.Type)\n\t\tif len(c.Authorization.Type) == 0 {\n\t\t\tc.Authorization.Type = \"Bearer\"\n\t\t}\n\t\tif strings.ToLower(c.Authorization.Type) == \"basic\" {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(`authorization type cannot be set to \"basic\", use \"basic_auth\" instead`)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif c.BasicAuth != nil || c.OAuth2 != nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth, oauth2 & authorization must be configured\")\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tif len(c.BearerToken) > 0 {\n\t\t\tc.Authorization = &Authorization{Credentials: c.BearerToken}\n\t\t\tc.Authorization.Type = \"Bearer\"\n\t\t\tc.BearerToken = \"\"\n\t\t}\n\t\tif len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n\t\t\tc.Authorization = &Authorization{CredentialsFile: c.BearerTokenFile}\n\t\t\tc.Authorization.Type = \"Bearer\"\n\t\t\tc.BearerTokenFile = \"\"\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif c.OAuth2 != nil {\n\t\tif c.BasicAuth != nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth, oauth2 & authorization must be configured\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tif len(c.OAuth2.ClientID) == 0 {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"oauth2 client_id must be configured\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tif len(c.OAuth2.TokenURL) == 0 {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"oauth2 token_url must be configured\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tif c.OAuth2.GrantType == grantTypeJWTBearer {\n\t\t\tif nonZeroCount(len(c.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKey) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyFile) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyRef) > 0) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of oauth2 client_certificate_key, client_certificate_key_file & client_certificate_key_ref must be configured using grant-type=urn:ietf:params:oauth:grant-type:jwt-bearer\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif c.OAuth2.SignatureAlgorithm != \"\" && !slices.Contains(validSignatureAlgorithm, c.OAuth2.SignatureAlgorithm) {\n\t\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"valid signature algorithms are RS256, RS384 and RS512\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if nonZeroCount(len(c.OAuth2.ClientSecret) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientSecretFile) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientSecretRef) > 0) > 1 {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of oauth2 client_secret, client_secret_file & client_secret_ref must be configured using grant-type=client_credentials\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif err := c.ProxyConfig.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\tif c.HTTPHeaders != nil {\n\t\tif err := c.HTTPHeaders.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\nfunc (c *HTTPClientConfig) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(interface{}) error) error {\n\ttype plain HTTPClientConfig\n\t*c = DefaultHTTPClientConfig\n\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(c)); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\treturn c.Validate()\n}\n\n// UnmarshalJSON implements the json.Marshaler interface for URL.\nfunc (c *HTTPClientConfig) UnmarshalJSON(data []byte) error {\n\ttype SecretManager\n}\n\n// HTTPClientOption defines an option that can be applied to the HTTP client.\ntype HTTPClientOption interface {\n\tapplyToHTTPClientOptions(options *httpClientOptions)\n}\n\ntype {\n\tsecretManager SecretManager\n}\n\nfunc (s *secretManagerOption) applyToHTTPClientOptions(opts *httpClientOptions) {\n\topts.secretManager = s.secretManager\n}\n\nfunc (s *secretManagerOption) &secretManagerOption{\n\t\tsecretManager: manager,\n\t}\n}\n\n// NewClient returns a http.Client using the specified http.RoundTripper.\nfunc newClient(rt http.RoundTripper) *http.Client {\n\treturn &http.Client{Transport: rt}\n}\n\n// NewClientFromConfig returns a new HTTP client configured for the\n// given config.HTTPClientConfig and config.HTTPClientOption.\n// The name is used as go-conntrack metric label.\nfunc NewClientFromConfig(cfg HTTPClientConfig, name string, optFuncs ...HTTPClientOption) (*http.Client, error) {\n\trt, err := NewRoundTripperFromConfig(cfg, name, optFuncs...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tclient := newClient(rt)\n\tif !cfg.FollowRedirects {\n\t\tclient.CheckRedirect = func(*http.Request, []*http.Request) error {\n\t\t\treturn http.ErrUseLastResponse\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn client, nil\n}\n\n// NewRoundTripperFromConfig returns a new HTTP RoundTripper configured for the\n// given config.HTTPClientConfig and config.HTTPClientOption.\n// The name is used as go-conntrack metric label.\nfunc NewRoundTripperFromConfig(cfg HTTPClientConfig, name string, optFuncs ...HTTPClientOption) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\treturn NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext(context.Background(), cfg, name, optFuncs...)\n}\n\n// NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext returns a new HTTP RoundTripper configured for the\n// given config.HTTPClientConfig and config.HTTPClientOption.\n// The name is used as go-conntrack metric label.\nfunc NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext(ctx context.Context, cfg HTTPClientConfig, name string, optFuncs ...HTTPClientOption) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\topts := defaultHTTPClientOptions\n\tfor _, opt := range optFuncs {\n\t\topt.applyToHTTPClientOptions(&opts)\n\t}\n\n\tvar dialContext func(ctx context.Context, network, addr string) (net.Conn, error)\n\n\tif opts.dialContextFunc != nil {\n\t\tdialContext = conntrack.NewDialContextFunc(\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithDialContextFunc((func(context.Context, string, string) (net.Conn, error))(opts.dialContextFunc)),\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithTracing(),\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithName(name))\n\t} else {\n\t\tdialContext = conntrack.NewDialContextFunc(\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithTracing(),\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithName(name))\n\t}\n\n\tnewRT := func(tlsConfig *tls.Config) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\t\t// The only timeout we care about is the configured scrape timeout.\n\t\t// It is applied on request. So we leave out any timings here.\n\t\tvar rt http.RoundTripper = &http.Transport{\n\t\t\tProxy:                 cfg.Proxy(),\n\t\t\tProxyConnectHeader:    cfg.GetProxyConnectHeader(),\n\t\t\tMaxIdleConns:          20000,\n\t\t\tMaxIdleConnsPerHost:   1000, // see https://github.com/golang/go/issues/13801\n\t\t\tDisableKeepAlives:     !opts.keepAlivesEnabled,\n\t\t\tTLSClientConfig:       tlsConfig,\n\t\t\tDisableCompression:    true,\n\t\t\tIdleConnTimeout:       opts.idleConnTimeout,\n\t\t\tTLSHandshakeTimeout:   10 * time.Second,\n\t\t\tExpectContinueTimeout: 1 * time.Second,\n\t\t\tDialContext:           dialContext,\n\t\t}\n\t\tif opts.http2Enabled && cfg.EnableHTTP2 {\n\t\t\thttp2t, err := http2.ConfigureTransports(rt.(*http.Transport))\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\thttp2t.ReadIdleTimeout = time.Minute\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If a authorization_credentials is provided, create a round tripper that will set the\n\t\t// Authorization header correctly on each request.\n\t\tif cfg.Authorization != nil {\n\t\t\tcredentialsSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.Authorization.Credentials, cfg.Authorization.CredentialsFile, cfg.Authorization.CredentialsRef)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use credentials: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt = NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper(cfg.Authorization.Type, credentialsSecret, rt)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Backwards compatibility, be nice with importers who would not have\n\t\t// called Validate().\n\t\tif len(cfg.BearerToken) > 0 || len(cfg.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n\t\t\tbearerSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.BearerToken, cfg.BearerTokenFile, \"\")\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use bearer token: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt = NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper(\"Bearer\", bearerSecret, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif cfg.BasicAuth != nil {\n\t\t\tusernameSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, Secret(cfg.BasicAuth.Username), cfg.BasicAuth.UsernameFile, cfg.BasicAuth.UsernameRef)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use username: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tpasswordSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.BasicAuth.Password, cfg.BasicAuth.PasswordFile, cfg.BasicAuth.PasswordRef)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use password: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt = NewBasicAuthRoundTripper(usernameSecret, passwordSecret, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif cfg.OAuth2 != nil {\n\t\t\tvar (\n\t\t\t\toauthCredential SecretReader\n\t\t\t\terr             error\n\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t\tif cfg.OAuth2.GrantType == grantTypeJWTBearer {\n\t\t\t\toauthCredential, err = toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKey, cfg.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyFile, cfg.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyRef)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use client certificate: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\toauthCredential, err = toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.OAuth2.ClientSecret, cfg.OAuth2.ClientSecretFile, cfg.OAuth2.ClientSecretRef)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use client secret: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt = NewOAuth2RoundTripper(oauthCredential, cfg.OAuth2, rt, &opts)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif cfg.HTTPHeaders != nil {\n\t\t\trt = NewHeadersRoundTripper(cfg.HTTPHeaders, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif opts.userAgent != \"\" {\n\t\t\trt = NewUserAgentRoundTripper(opts.userAgent, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif opts.host != \"\" {\n\t\t\trt = NewHostRoundTripper(opts.host, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Return a new configured RoundTripper.\n\t\treturn rt, nil\n\t}\n\n\ttlsConfig, err := opts.newTLSConfigFunc(ctx, &cfg.TLSConfig, WithSecretManager(opts.secretManager))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\ttlsSettings, err := cfg.TLSConfig.roundTripperSettings(opts.secretManager)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif tlsSettings.immutable() {\n\t\t// No need for a RoundTripper that reloads the files automatically.\n\t\treturn newRT(tlsConfig)\n\t}\n\treturn NewTLSRoundTripperWithContext(ctx, tlsConfig, tlsSettings, newRT)\n}\n\n// SecretManager manages secret data mapped to names known as \"references\" or \"refs\".\ntype SecretManager interface {\n\t// Fetch returns the secret data given a secret name indicated by `secretRef`.\n\tFetch(ctx context.Context, secretRef string) (string, error)\n}\n\ntype SecretReader interface {\n\tFetch(ctx context.Context) (string, error)\n\tDescription() string\n\tImmutable() bool\n}\n\ntype InlineSecret struct {\n\ttext string\n}\n\nfunc NewInlineSecret(text string) *InlineSecret {\n\treturn &InlineSecret{text: text}\n}\n\nfunc (s *InlineSecret) Fetch(context.Context) (string, error) {\n\treturn s.text, nil\n}\n\nfunc (*InlineSecret) Description() string {\n\treturn \"inline\"\n}\n\nfunc (*InlineSecret) Immutable() bool {\n\treturn true\n}\n\ntype FileSecret struct {\n\tfile string\n}\n\nfunc NewFileSecret(file string) *FileSecret {\n\treturn &FileSecret{file: file}\n}\n\nfunc (s *FileSecret) Fetch(context.Context) (string, error) {\n\tfileBytes, err := os.ReadFile(s.file)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read file %s: %w\", s.file, err)\n\t}\n\treturn strings.TrimSpace(string(fileBytes)), nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *FileSecret) Description() string {\n\treturn \"file \" + s.file\n}\n\nfunc (*FileSecret) Immutable() bool {\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// refSecret fetches a single secret from a SecretManager.\ntype refSecret struct {\n\tref     string\n\tmanager SecretManager // manager is expected to be not nil.\n}\n\nfunc (s *refSecret) Fetch(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {\n\treturn s.manager.Fetch(ctx, s.ref)\n}\n\nfunc (s *refSecret) Description() string {\n\treturn \"ref \" + s.ref\n}\n\nfunc (*refSecret) Immutable() bool {\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// toSecret returns a SecretReader from one of the given sources, assuming exactly\n// one or none of the sources are provided.\nfunc toSecret(secretManager SecretManager, text Secret, file, ref string) (SecretReader, error) {\n\tif text != \"\" {\n\t\treturn NewInlineSecret(string(text)), nil\n\t}\n\tif file != \"\" {\n\t\treturn NewFileSecret(file), nil\n\t}\n\tif ref != \"\" {\n\t\tif secretManager == nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"cannot use secret ref without manager\")\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn &refSecret{\n\t\t\tref:     ref,\n\t\t\tmanager: secretManager,\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\treturn nil, nil\n}\n\ntype authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper struct {\n\tauthType        string\n\tauthCredentials SecretReader\n\trt              http.RoundTripper\n}\n\n// NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper adds the authorization credentials\n// read from the provided SecretReader to a request unless the authorization header\n// has already been set.\nfunc NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper(authType string, authCredentials SecretReader, rt http.RoundTripper) http.RoundTripper {\n\treturn &authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper{authType, authCredentials, rt}\n}\n\nfunc (rt *authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tif len(req.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")) != 0 {\n\t\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n\t}\n\n\tvar authCredentials string\n\tif rt.authCredentials != nil {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tauthCredentials, err = rt.authCredentials.Fetch(req.Context())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read authorization credentials: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treq = cloneRequest(req)\n\treq.Header.Set(\"Authorization\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %s\", rt.authType, authCredentials))\n\n\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nfunc (rt *authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n\tif ci, ok := rt.rt.(closeIdler); ok {\n\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n}\n\ntype basicAuthRoundTripper struct {\n\tusername SecretReader\n\tpassword SecretReader\n\trt       http.RoundTripper\n}\n\n// NewBasicAuthRoundTripper will apply a BASIC auth authorization header to a request unless it has\n// already been set.\nfunc NewBasicAuthRoundTripper(username, password SecretReader, rt http.RoundTripper) http.RoundTripper {\n\treturn &basicAuthRoundTripper{username, password, rt}\n}\n\nfunc (rt *basicAuthRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tif len(req.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")) != 0 {\n\t\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n\t}\n\tvar username string\n\tvar password string\n\tif rt.username != nil {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tusername, err = rt.username.Fetch(req.Context())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read basic auth username: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif rt.password != nil {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tpassword, err = rt.password.Fetch(req.Context())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read basic auth password: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treq = cloneRequest(req)\n\treq.SetBasicAuth(username, password)\n\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nfunc (rt *basicAuthRoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n\tif ci, ok := rt.rt.(closeIdler); ok {\n\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n}\n\ntype oauth2RoundTripper struct {\n\tmtx        sync.RWMutex\n\tlastRT     *oauth2.Transport\n\tlastSecret string\n\n\t// Required for interaction with Oauth2 server.\n\tconfig          *OAuth2\n\toauthCredential SecretReader\n\topts            *httpClientOptions\n\tclient          *http.Client\n}\n\nfunc NewOAuth2RoundTripper(oauthCredential SecretReader, config *OAuth2, next http.RoundTripper, opts *httpClientOptions) http.RoundTripper {\n\tif oauthCredential == nil {\n\t\toauthCredential = NewInlineSecret(\"\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn &oauth2RoundTripper{\n\t\tconfig: config,\n\t\t// A correct tokenSource will be added later on.\n\t\tlastRT:          &oauth2.Transport{Base: next},\n\t\topts:            opts,\n\t\toauthCredential: oauthCredential,\n\t}\n}\n\ntype oauth2TokenSourceConfig interface {\n\tTokenSource(ctx context.Context) oauth2.TokenSource\n}\n\nfunc (rt *oauth2RoundTripper) newOauth2TokenSource(req *http.Request, clientCredential string) (client *http.Client, source oauth2.TokenSource, err error) {\n\ttlsConfig, err := NewTLSConfig(&rt.config.TLSConfig, WithSecretManager(rt.opts.secretManager))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n\t}\n\n\ttlsTransport := func(tlsConfig *tls.Config) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\t\treturn &http.Transport{\n\t\t\tTLSClientConfig:       tlsConfig,\n\t\t\tProxy:                 rt.config.Proxy(),\n\t\t\tProxyConnectHeader:    rt.config.GetProxyConnectHeader(),\n\t\t\tDisableKeepAlives:     !rt.opts.keepAlivesEnabled,\n\t\t\tMaxIdleConns:          20,\n\t\t\tMaxIdleConnsPerHost:   1, // see https://github.com/golang/go/issues/13801\n\t\t\tIdleConnTimeout:       10 * time.Second,\n\t\t\tTLSHandshakeTimeout:   10 * time.Second,\n\t\t\tExpectContinueTimeout: 1 * time.Second,\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar t http.RoundTripper\n\ttlsSettings, err := rt.config.TLSConfig.roundTripperSettings(rt.opts.secretManager)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n\t}\n\tif tlsSettings.immutable() {\n\t\tt, _ = tlsTransport(tlsConfig)\n\t} else {\n\t\tt, err = NewTLSRoundTripperWithContext(req.Context(), tlsConfig, tlsSettings, tlsTransport)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif ua := req.UserAgent(); ua != \"\" {\n\t\tt = NewUserAgentRoundTripper(ua, t)\n\t}\n\n\tvar config oauth2TokenSourceConfig\n\n\tif rt.config.GrantType == grantTypeJWTBearer {\n\t\t// RFC 7523 3.1 - JWT authorization grants\n\t\t// RFC 7523 3.2 - Client Authentication Processing is not implement upstream yet,\n\t\t// see https://github.com/golang/oauth2/pull/745\n\n\t\tvar sig *jwt.SigningMethodRSA\n\t\tswitch rt.config.SignatureAlgorithm {\n\t\tcase jwt.SigningMethodRS256.Name:\n\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS256\n\t\tcase jwt.SigningMethodRS384.Name:\n\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS384\n\t\tcase jwt.SigningMethodRS512.Name:\n\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS512\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS256\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tiss := rt.config.Iss\n\t\tif iss == \"\" {\n\t\t\tiss = rt.config.ClientID\n\t\t}\n\t\tconfig = &JwtGrantTypeConfig{\n\t\t\tPrivateKey:       []byte(clientCredential),\n\t\t\tPrivateKeyID:     rt.config.ClientCertificateKeyID,\n\t\t\tScopes:           rt.config.Scopes,\n\t\t\tTokenURL:         rt.config.TokenURL,\n\t\t\tSigningAlgorithm: sig,\n\t\t\tIss:              iss,\n\t\t\tSubject:          rt.config.ClientID,\n\t\t\tAudience:         rt.config.Audience,\n\t\t\tPrivateClaims:    rt.config.Claims,\n\t\t\tEndpointParams:   mapToValues(rt.config.EndpointParams),\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tconfig = &clientcredentials.Config{\n\t\t\tClientID:       rt.config.ClientID,\n\t\t\tClientSecret:   clientCredential,\n\t\t\tScopes:         rt.config.Scopes,\n\t\t\tTokenURL:       rt.config.TokenURL,\n\t\t\tEndpointParams: mapToValues(rt.config.EndpointParams),\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tclient = &http.Client{Transport: t}\n\tctx := context.WithValue(context.Background(), oauth2.HTTPClient, client)\n\treturn client, config.TokenSource(ctx), nil\n}\n\nfunc (rt *oauth2RoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tsecret    string\n\t\tneedsInit bool\n\t)\n\n\trt.mtx.RLock()\n\tsecret = rt.lastSecret\n\tneedsInit = rt.lastRT.Source == nil\n\trt.mtx.RUnlock()\n\n\t// Fetch the secret if it's our first run or always if the secret can change.\n\tif !rt.oauthCredential.Immutable() || needsInit {\n\t\tnewSecret, err := rt.oauthCredential.Fetch(req.Context())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read oauth2 client secret: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif newSecret != secret || needsInit {\n\t\t\t// Secret changed or it's a first run. Rebuilt oauth2 setup.\n\t\t\tclient, source, err := rt.newOauth2TokenSource(req, newSecret)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\trt.mtx.Lock()\n\t\t\trt.lastSecret = newSecret\n\t\t\trt.lastRT.Source = source\n\t\t\tif rt.client != nil {\n\t\t\t\trt.client.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt.client = client\n\t\t\trt.mtx.Unlock()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\trt.mtx.RLock()\n\tcurrentRT := rt.lastRT\n\trt.mtx.RUnlock()\n\treturn currentRT.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nfunc (rt *oauth2RoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n\tif rt.client != nil {\n\t\trt.client.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n\tif ci, ok := rt.lastRT.Base.(closeIdler); ok {\n\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc mapToValues(m map[string]string) url.Values {\n\tv := url.Values{}\n\tfor name, value := range m {\n\t\tv.Set(name, value)\n\t}\n\n\treturn v\n}\n\n// cloneRequest returns a clone of the provided *http.Request.\n// The clone is a shallow copy of the struct and its Header map.\nfunc cloneRequest(r *http.Request) *http.Request {\n\t// Shallow copy of the struct.\n\tr2 := new(http.Request)\n\t*r2 = *r\n\t// Deep copy of the Header.\n\tr2.Header = make(http.Header)\n\tfor k, s := range r.Header {\n\t\tr2.Header[k] = s\n\t}\n\treturn r2\n}\n\ntype tlsConfigOptions struct {\n\tsecretManager SecretManager\n}\n\n// TLSConfigOption defines an option that can be applied to the HTTP client.\ntype TLSConfigOption interface {\n\tapplyToTLSConfigOptions(options *tlsConfigOptions)\n}\n\n// NewTLSConfig creates a new tls.Config from the given TLSConfig.\nfunc NewTLSConfig(cfg *TLSConfig, optFuncs ...TLSConfigOption) (*tls.Config, error) {\n\treturn NewTLSConfigWithContext(context.Background(), cfg, optFuncs...)\n}\n\n// NewTLSConfigWithContext creates a new tls.Config from the given TLSConfig.\nfunc NewTLSConfigWithContext(ctx context.Context, cfg *TLSConfig, optFuncs ...TLSConfigOption) (*tls.Config, error) {\n\topts := tlsConfigOptions{}\n\tfor _, opt := range optFuncs {\n\t\topt.applyToTLSConfigOptions(&opts)\n\t}\n\n\tif err := cfg.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\ttlsConfig := &tls.Config{\n\t\tInsecureSkipVerify: cfg.InsecureSkipVerify,\n\t\tMinVersion:         uint16(cfg.MinVersion),\n\t\tMaxVersion:         uint16(cfg.MaxVersion),\n\t}\n\n\tif cfg.MaxVersion != 0 && cfg.MinVersion != 0 {\n\t\tif cfg.MaxVersion < cfg.MinVersion {\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"tls_config.max_version must be greater than or equal to tls_config.min_version if both are specified\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// If a CA cert is provided then let's read it in so we can validate the\n\t// scrape target's certificate properly.\n\tcaSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, Secret(cfg.CA), cfg.CAFile, cfg.CARef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use CA cert: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tif caSecret != nil {\n\t\tca, err := caSecret.Fetch(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read CA cert: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !updateRootCA(tlsConfig, []byte(ca)) {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use specified CA cert %s\", caSecret.Description())\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(cfg.ServerName) > 0 {\n\t\ttlsConfig.ServerName = cfg.ServerName\n\t}\n\n\t// If a client cert & key is provided then configure TLS config accordingly.\n\tif cfg.usingClientCert() && cfg.usingClientKey() {\n\t\t// Verify that client cert and key are valid.\n\t\tif _, err := cfg.getClientCertificate(ctx, opts.secretManager); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\ttlsConfig.GetClientCertificate = func(cri *tls.CertificateRequestInfo) (*tls.Certificate, error) {\n\t\t\tvar ctx context.Context\n\t\t\tif cri != nil {\n\t\t\t\tctx = cri.Context()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn cfg.getClientCertificate(ctx, opts.secretManager)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn tlsConfig, nil\n}\n\n// TLSConfig configures the options for TLS connections.\ntype TLSConfig struct {\n\t// Text of the CA cert to use for the targets.\n\tCA string `yaml:\"ca,omitempty\" json:\"ca,omitempty\"`\n\t// Text of the client cert file for the targets.\n\tCert string `yaml:\"cert,omitempty\" json:\"cert,omitempty\"`\n\t// Text of the client key file for the targets.\n\tKey Secret `yaml:\"key,omitempty\" json:\"key,omitempty\"`\n\t// The CA cert to use for the targets.\n\tCAFile string `yaml:\"ca_file,omitempty\" json:\"ca_file,omitempty\"`\n\t// The client cert file for the targets.\n\tCertFile string `yaml:\"cert_file,omitempty\" json:\"cert_file,omitempty\"`\n\t// The client key file for the targets.\n\tKeyFile string `yaml:\"key_file,omitempty\" json:\"key_file,omitempty\"`\n\t// CARef is the name of the secret within the secret manager to use as the CA cert for the\n\t// targets.\n\tCARef string `yaml:\"ca_ref,omitempty\" json:\"ca_ref,omitempty\"`\n\t// CertRef is the name of the secret within the secret manager to use as the client cert for\n\t// the targets.\n\tCertRef string `yaml:\"cert_ref,omitempty\" json:\"cert_ref,omitempty\"`\n\t// KeyRef is the name of the secret within the secret manager to use as the client key for\n\t// the targets.\n\tKeyRef string `yaml:\"key_ref,omitempty\" json:\"key_ref,omitempty\"`\n\t// Used to verify the hostname for the targets.\n\tServerName string `yaml:\"server_name,omitempty\" json:\"server_name,omitempty\"`\n\t// Disable target certificate validation.\n\tInsecureSkipVerify bool `yaml:\"insecure_skip_verify\" json:\"insecure_skip_verify\"`\n\t// Minimum TLS version.\n\tMinVersion TLSVersion `yaml:\"min_version,omitempty\" json:\"min_version,omitempty\"`\n\t// Maximum TLS version.\n\tMaxVersion TLSVersion `yaml:\"max_version,omitempty\" json:\"max_version,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\nfunc (c *TLSConfig) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n\tif c == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tc.CAFile = JoinDir(dir, c.CAFile)\n\tc.CertFile = JoinDir(dir, c.CertFile)\n\tc.KeyFile = JoinDir(dir, c.KeyFile)\n}\n\n// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\nfunc (c *TLSConfig) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(interface{}) error) error {\n\ttype plain TLSConfig\n\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(c)); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\treturn c.Validate()\n}\n\n// Validate validates the TLSConfig to check that only one of the inlined or\n// file-based fields for the TLS CA, client certificate, and client key are\n// used.\nfunc (c *TLSConfig) Validate() error {\n\tif nonZeroCount(len(c.CA) > 0, len(c.CAFile) > 0, len(c.CARef) > 0) > 1 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of ca, ca_file & ca_ref must be configured\")\n\t}\n\tif nonZeroCount(len(c.Cert) > 0, len(c.CertFile) > 0, len(c.CertRef) > 0) > 1 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of cert, cert_file & cert_ref must be configured\")\n\t}\n\tif nonZeroCount(len(c.Key) > 0, len(c.KeyFile) > 0, len(c.KeyRef) > 0) > 1 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of key and key_file must be configured\")\n\t}\n\n\tif c.usingClientCert() && !c.usingClientKey() {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"exactly one of key or key_file must be configured when a client certificate is configured\")\n\t} else if c.usingClientKey() && !c.usingClientCert() {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"exactly one of cert or cert_file must be configured when a client key is configured\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *TLSConfig) usingClientCert() bool {\n\treturn len(c.Cert) > 0 || len(c.CertFile) > 0 || len(c.CertRef) > 0\n}\n\nfunc (c *TLSConfig) usingClientKey() bool {\n\treturn len(c.Key) > 0 || len(c.KeyFile) > 0 || len(c.KeyRef) > 0\n}\n\nfunc (c *TLSConfig) roundTripperSettings(secretManager SecretManager) (TLSRoundTripperSettings, error) {\n\tca, err := toSecret(secretManager, Secret(c.CA), c.CAFile, c.CARef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn TLSRoundTripperSettings{}, err\n\t}\n\tcert, err := toSecret(secretManager, Secret(c.Cert), c.CertFile, c.CertRef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn TLSRoundTripperSettings{}, err\n\t}\n\tkey, err := toSecret(secretManager, c.Key, c.KeyFile, c.KeyRef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn TLSRoundTripperSettings{}, err\n\t}\n\treturn TLSRoundTripperSettings{\n\t\tCA:   ca,\n\t\tCert: cert,\n\t\tKey:  key,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\n// getClientCertificate reads the pair of client cert and key and returns a tls.Certificate.\nfunc (c *TLSConfig) getClientCertificate(ctx context.Context, secretManager SecretManager) (*tls.Certificate, error) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tcertData, keyData string\n\t\terr               error\n\t)\n\n\tcertSecret, err := toSecret(secretManager, Secret(c.Cert), c.CertFile, c.CertRef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use client cert: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tif certSecret != nil {\n\t\tcertData, err = certSecret.Fetch(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read specified client cert: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tkeySecret, err := toSecret(secretManager, c.Key, c.KeyFile, c.KeyRef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use client key: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tif keySecret != nil {\n\t\tkeyData, err = keySecret.Fetch(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read specified client key: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tcert, err := tls.X509KeyPair([]byte(certData), []byte(keyData))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use specified client cert (%s) & key (%s): %w\", certSecret.Description(), keySecret.Description(), err)\n\t}\n\n\treturn &cert, nil\n}\n\n// updateRootCA parses the given byte slice as a series of PEM encoded certificates and updates tls.Config.RootCAs.\nfunc updateRootCA(cfg *tls.Config, b []byte) bool {\n\tcaCertPool := x509.NewCertPool()\n\tif !caCertPool.AppendCertsFromPEM(b) {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tcfg.RootCAs = caCertPool\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// tlsRoundTripper is a RoundTripper that updates automatically its TLS\n// configuration whenever the content of the CA file changes.\ntype tlsRoundTripper struct {\n\tsettings TLSRoundTripperSettings\n\n\t// newRT returns a new RoundTripper.\n\tnewRT func(*tls.Config) (http.RoundTripper, error)\n\n\tmtx          sync.RWMutex\n\trt           http.RoundTripper\n\thashCAData   []byte\n\thashCertData []byte\n\thashKeyData  []byte\n\ttlsConfig    *tls.Config\n}\n\ntype TLSRoundTripperSettings struct {\n\tCA   SecretReader\n\tCert SecretReader\n\tKey  SecretReader\n}\n\nfunc (t *TLSRoundTripperSettings) immutable() bool {\n\treturn (t.CA == nil || t.CA.Immutable()) && (t.Cert == nil || t.Cert.Immutable()) && (t.Key == nil || t.Key.Immutable())\n}\n\nfunc NewTLSRoundTripper(\n\tcfg *tls.Config,\n\tsettings TLSRoundTripperSettings,\n\tnewRT func(*tls.Config) (http.RoundTripper, error),\n) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\treturn NewTLSRoundTripperWithContext(context.Background(), cfg, settings, newRT)\n}\n\nfunc NewTLSRoundTripperWithContext(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tcfg *tls.Config,\n\tsettings TLSRoundTripperSettings,\n\tnewRT func(*tls.Config) (http.RoundTripper, error),\n) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\tt := &tlsRoundTripper{\n\t\tsettings:  settings,\n\t\tnewRT:     newRT,\n\t\ttlsConfig: cfg,\n\t}\n\n\trt, err := t.newRT(t.tlsConfig)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tt.rt = rt\n\t_, t.hashCAData, t.hashCertData, t.hashKeyData, err = t.getTLSDataWithHash(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn t, nil\n}\n\nfunc (t *tlsRoundTripper) getTLSDataWithHash(ctx context.Context) ([]byte, []byte, []byte, []byte, error) {\n\tvar caBytes, certBytes, keyBytes []byte\n\n\tif t.settings.CA != nil {\n\t\tca, err := t.settings.CA.Fetch(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil, nil, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read CA cert: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tcaBytes = []byte(ca)\n\t}\n\n\tif t.settings.Cert != nil {\n\t\tcert, err := t.settings.Cert.Fetch(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil, nil, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read client cert: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tcertBytes = []byte(cert)\n\t}\n\n\tif t.settings.Key != nil {\n\t\tkey, err := t.settings.Key.Fetch(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil, nil, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read client key: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tkeyBytes = []byte(key)\n\t}\n\n\tvar caHash, certHash, keyHash [32]byte\n\n\tif len(caBytes) > 0 {\n\t\tcaHash = sha256.Sum256(caBytes)\n\t}\n\tif len(certBytes) > 0 {\n\t\tcertHash = sha256.Sum256(certBytes)\n\t}\n\tif len(keyBytes) > 0 {\n\t\tkeyHash = sha256.Sum256(keyBytes)\n\t}\n\n\treturn caBytes, caHash[:], certHash[:], keyHash[:], nil\n}\n\n// RoundTrip implements the http.RoundTrip interface.\nfunc (t *tlsRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tcaData, caHash, certHash, keyHash, err := t.getTLSDataWithHash(req.Context())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tt.mtx.RLock()\n\tequal := bytes.Equal(caHash, t.hashCAData) &&\n\t\tbytes.Equal(certHash, t.hashCertData) &&\n\t\tbytes.Equal(keyHash, t.hashKeyData)\n\trt := t.rt\n\tt.mtx.RUnlock()\n\tif equal {\n\t\t// The CA cert hasn't changed, use the existing RoundTripper.\n\t\treturn rt.RoundTrip(req)\n\t}\n\n\t// Create a new RoundTripper.\n\t// The cert and key files are read separately by the client\n\t// using GetClientCertificate.\n\ttlsConfig := t.tlsConfig.Clone()\n\tif !updateRootCA(tlsConfig, caData) {\n\t\tif t.settings.CA == nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"unable to use specified CA cert: none configured\")\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use specified CA cert %s\", t.settings.CA.Description())\n\t}\n\trt, err = t.newRT(tlsConfig)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tt.CloseIdleConnections()\n\n\tt.mtx.Lock()\n\tt.rt = rt\n\tt.hashCAData = caHash\n\tt.hashCertData = certHash\n\tt.hashKeyData = keyHash\n\tt.mtx.Unlock()\n\n\treturn rt.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nfunc (t *tlsRoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n\tt.mtx.RLock()\n\tdefer t.mtx.RUnlock()\n\tif ci, ok := t.rt.(closeIdler); ok {\n\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n}\n\ntype userAgentRoundTripper struct {\n\tuserAgent string\n\trt        http.RoundTripper\n}\n\ntype hostRoundTripper struct {\n\thost string\n\trt   http.RoundTripper\n}\n\n// NewUserAgentRoundTripper adds the user agent every request header.\nfunc NewUserAgentRoundTripper(userAgent string, rt http.RoundTripper) http.RoundTripper {\n\treturn &userAgentRoundTripper{userAgent, rt}\n}\n\n// NewHostRoundTripper sets the [http.Request.Host] of every request.\nfunc NewHostRoundTripper(host string, rt http.RoundTripper) http.RoundTripper {\n\treturn &hostRoundTripper{host, rt}\n}\n\nfunc (rt *userAgentRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\treq = cloneRequest(req)\n\treq.Header.Set(\"User-Agent\", rt.userAgent)\n\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nfunc (rt *userAgentRoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n\tif ci, ok := rt.rt.(closeIdler); ok {\n\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (rt *hostRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\treq = cloneRequest(req)\n\treq.Host = rt.host\n\treq.Header.Set(\"Host\", rt.host)\n\treturn err != nil {\n   293→\t\treturn err\n   294→\t}\n   295→\treturn o.Validate()\n   296→}\n   297→\n   298→// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\n   299→func (o *OAuth2) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n   300→\tif o == nil {\n   301→\t\treturn\n   302→\t}\n   303→\to.ClientSecretFile = JoinDir(dir, o.ClientSecretFile)\n   304→\to.TLSConfig.SetDirectory(dir)\n   305→}\n   306→\n   307→// LoadHTTPConfig parses the YAML input s into a HTTPClientConfig.\n   308→func LoadHTTPConfig(s string) (*HTTPClientConfig, error) {\n   309→\tcfg := &HTTPClientConfig{}\n   310→\terr := yaml.UnmarshalStrict([]byte(s), cfg)\n   311→\tif err != nil {\n   312→\t\treturn nil, err\n   313→\t}\n   314→\treturn cfg, nil\n   315→}\n   316→\n   317→// LoadHTTPConfigFile parses the given YAML file into a HTTPClientConfig.\n   318→func LoadHTTPConfigFile(filename string) (*HTTPClientConfig, []byte, error) {\n   319→\tcontent, err := os.ReadFile(filename)\n   320→\tif err != nil {\n   321→\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   322→\t}\n   323→\tcfg, err := LoadHTTPConfig(string(content))\n   324→\tif err != nil {\n   325→\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   326→\t}\n   327→\tcfg.SetDirectory(filepath.Dir(filepath.Dir(filename)))\n   328→\treturn cfg, content, nil\n   329→}\n   330→\n   331→// HTTPClientConfig configures an HTTP client.\n   332→type HTTPClientConfig struct {\n   333→\t// The HTTP basic authentication credentials for the targets.\n   334→\tBasicAuth *BasicAuth `yaml:\"basic_auth,omitempty\" json:\"basic_auth,omitempty\"`\n   335→\t// The HTTP authorization credentials for the targets.\n   336→\tAuthorization *Authorization `yaml:\"authorization,omitempty\" json:\"authorization,omitempty\"`\n   337→\t// The OAuth2 client credentials used to fetch a token for the targets.\n   338→\tOAuth2 *OAuth2 `yaml:\"oauth2,omitempty\" json:\"oauth2,omitempty\"`\n   339→\t// The bearer token for the targets. Deprecated in favour of\n   340→\t// Authorization.Credentials.\n   341→\tBearerToken Secret `yaml:\"bearer_token,omitempty\" json:\"bearer_token,omitempty\"`\n   342→\t// The bearer token file for the targets. Deprecated in favour of\n   343→\t// Authorization.CredentialsFile.\n   344→\tBearerTokenFile string `yaml:\"bearer_token_file,omitempty\" json:\"bearer_token_file,omitempty\"`\n   345→\t// TLSConfig to use to connect to the targets.\n   346→\tTLSConfig TLSConfig `yaml:\"tls_config,omitempty\" json:\"tls_config,omitempty\"`\n   347→\t// FollowRedirects specifies whether the client should follow HTTP 3xx redirects.\n   348→\t// The omitempty flag is not set, because it would be hidden from the\n   349→\t// marshalled configuration when set to false.\n   350→\tFollowRedirects bool `yaml:\"follow_redirects\" json:\"follow_redirects\"`\n   351→\t// EnableHTTP2 specifies whether the client should configure HTTP2.\n   352→\t// The omitempty flag is not set, because it would be hidden from the\n   353→\t// marshalled configuration when set to false.\n   354→\tEnableHTTP2 bool `yaml:\"enable_http2\" json:\"enable_http2\"`\n   355→\t// Proxy configuration.\n   356→\tProxyConfig `yaml:\",inline\"`\n   357→\t// HTTPHeaders specify headers to inject in the requests. Those headers\n   358→\t// could be marshalled back to the users.\n   359→\tHTTPHeaders *Headers `yaml:\"http_headers,omitempty\" json:\"http_headers,omitempty\"`\n   360→}\n   361→\n   362→// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\n   363→func (c *HTTPClientConfig) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n   364→\tif c == nil {\n   365→\t\treturn\n   366→\t}\n   367→\tc.TLSConfig.SetDirectory(dir)\n   368→\tc.BasicAuth.SetDirectory(dir)\n   369→\tc.Authorization.SetDirectory(dir)\n   370→\tc.OAuth2.SetDirectory(dir)\n   371→\tc.HTTPHeaders.SetDirectory(dir)\n   372→\tc.BearerTokenFile = JoinDir(dir, c.BearerTokenFile)\n   373→}\n   374→\n   375→// nonZeroCount returns the amount of values that are non-zero.\n   376→func nonZeroCount[T comparable](values ...T) int {\n   377→\tcount := 0\n   378→\tvar zero T\n   379→\tfor _, value := range values {\n   380→\t\tif value != zero {\n   381→\t\t\tcount++\n   382→\t\t}\n   383→\t}\n   384→\treturn count\n   385→}\n   386→\n   387→// Validate validates the HTTPClientConfig to check only one of BearerToken,\n   388→// BasicAuth and BearerTokenFile is configured. It also validates that ProxyURL\n   389→// is set if ProxyConnectHeader is set.\n   390→func (c *HTTPClientConfig) Validate() error {\n   391→\t// Backwards compatibility with the bearer_token field.\n   392→\tif len(c.BearerToken) > 0 && len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n   393→\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of bearer_token & bearer_token_file must be configured\")\n   394→\t}\n   395→\tif (c.BasicAuth != nil || c.OAuth2 != nil) && (len(c.BearerToken) > 0 || len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0) {\n   396→\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth, oauth2, bearer_token & bearer_token_file must be configured\")\n   397→\t}\n   398→\tif c.BasicAuth != nil && nonZeroCount(c.BasicAuth.Username != \"\", c.BasicAuth.UsernameFile != \"\", c.BasicAuth.UsernameRef != \"\") > 1 {\n   399→\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth username, username_file & username_ref must be configured\")\n   400→\t}\n   401→\tif c.BasicAuth != nil && nonZeroCount(string(c.BasicAuth.Password) != \"\", c.BasicAuth.PasswordFile != \"\", c.BasicAuth.PasswordRef != \"\") > 1 {\n   402→\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth password, password_file & password_ref must be configured\")\n   403→\t}\n   404→\tif c.Authorization != nil {\n   405→\t\tif len(c.BearerToken) > 0 || len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n   406→\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"authorization is not compatible with bearer_token & bearer_token_file\")\n   407→\t\t}\n   408→\t\tif nonZeroCount(string(c.Authorization.Credentials) != \"\", c.Authorization.CredentialsFile != \"\", c.Authorization.CredentialsRef != \"\") > 1 {\n   409→\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of authorization credentials & credentials_file must be configured\")\n   410→\t\t}\n   411→\t\tc.Authorization.Type = strings.TrimSpace(c.Authorization.Type)\n   412→\t\tif len(c.Authorization.Type) == 0 {\n   413→\t\t\tc.Authorization.Type = \"Bearer\"\n   414→\t\t}\n   415→\t\tif strings.ToLower(c.Authorization.Type) == \"basic\" {\n   416→\t\t\treturn errors.New(`authorization type cannot be set to \"basic\", use \"basic_auth\" instead`)\n   417→\t\t}\n   418→\t\tif c.BasicAuth != nil || c.OAuth2 != nil {\n   419→\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth, oauth2 & authorization must be configured\")\n   420→\t\t}\n   421→\t} else {\n   422→\t\tif len(c.BearerToken) > 0 {\n   423→\t\t\tc.Authorization = &Authorization{Credentials: c.BearerToken}\n   424→\t\t\tc.Authorization.Type = \"Bearer\"\n   425→\t\t\tc.BearerToken = \"\"\n   426→\t\t}\n   427→\t\tif len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n   428→\t\t\tc.Authorization = &Authorization{CredentialsFile: c.BearerTokenFile}\n   429→\t\t\tc.Authorization.Type = \"Bearer\"\n   430→\t\t\tc.BearerTokenFile = \"\"\n   431→\t\t}\n   432→\t}\n   433→\tif c.OAuth2 != nil {\n   434→\t\tif c.BasicAuth != nil {\n   435→\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth, oauth2 & authorization must be configured\")\n   436→\t\t}\n   437→\t\tif len(c.OAuth2.ClientID) == 0 {\n   438→\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"oauth2 client_id must be configured\")\n   439→\t\t}\n   440→\t\tif len(c.OAuth2.TokenURL) == 0 {\n   441→\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"oauth2 token_url must be configured\")\n   442→\t\t}\n   443→\t\tif c.OAuth2.GrantType == grantTypeJWTBearer {\n   444→\t\t\tif nonZeroCount(len(c.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKey) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyFile) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyRef) > 0) > 1 {\n   445→\t\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of oauth2 client_certificate_key, client_certificate_key_file & client_certificate_key_ref must be configured using grant-type=urn:ietf:params:oauth:grant-type:jwt-bearer\")\n   446→\t\t\t}\n   447→\t\t\tif c.OAuth2.SignatureAlgorithm != \"\" && !slices.Contains(validSignatureAlgorithm, c.OAuth2.SignatureAlgorithm) {\n   448→\t\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"valid signature algorithms are RS256, RS384 and RS512\")\n   449→\t\t\t}\n   450→\t\t} else if nonZeroCount(len(c.OAuth2.ClientSecret) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientSecretFile) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientSecretRef) > 0) > 1 {\n   451→\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of oauth2 client_secret, client_secret_file & client_secret_ref must be configured using grant-type=client_credentials\")\n   452→\t\t}\n   453→\t}\n   454→\tif err := c.ProxyConfig.Validate(); err != nil {\n   455→\t\treturn err\n   456→\t}\n   457→\tif c.HTTPHeaders != nil {\n   458→\t\tif err := c.HTTPHeaders.Validate(); err != nil {\n   459→\t\t\treturn err\n   460→\t\t}\n   461→\t}\n   462→\treturn nil\n   463→}\n   464→\n   465→// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\n   466→func (c *HTTPClientConfig) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(interface{}) error) error {\n   467→\ttype plain HTTPClientConfig\n   468→\t*c = DefaultHTTPClientConfig\n   469→\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(c)); err != nil {\n   470→\t\treturn err\n   471→\t}\n   472→\treturn c.Validate()\n   473→}\n   474→\n   475→// UnmarshalJSON implements the json.Marshaler interface for URL.\n   476→func (c *HTTPClientConfig) UnmarshalJSON(data []byte) error {\n   477→\ttype plain HTTPClientConfig\n   478→\t*c = DefaultHTTPClientConfig\n   479→\tif err := json.Unmarshal(data, (*plain)(c)); err != nil {\n   480→\t\treturn err\n   481→\t}\n   482→\treturn c.Validate()\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\n   486→func (a *BasicAuth) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(interface{}) error) error {\n   487→\ttype plain BasicAuth\n   488→\treturn unmarshal((*plain)(a))\n   489→}\n   490→\n   491→// DialContextFunc defines the signature of the DialContext() function implemented\n   492→// by net.Dialer.\n   493→type DialContextFunc func(context.Context, string, string) (net.Conn, error)\n   494→\n   495→// NewTLSConfigFunc returns tls.Config.\n   496→type NewTLSConfigFunc func(context.Context, *TLSConfig, ...TLSConfigOption) (*tls.Config, error)\n   497→\n   498→type httpClientOptions struct {\n   499→\tdialContextFunc   DialContextFunc\n   500→\tnewTLSConfigFunc  NewTLSConfigFunc\n   501→\tkeepAlivesEnabled bool\n   502→\thttp2Enabled      bool\n   503→\tidleConnTimeout   time.Duration\n   504→\tuserAgent         string\n   505→\thost              string\n   506→\tsecretManager 569→\t})\n   570→}\n   571→\n   572→type secretManagerOption struct {\n   573→\tsecretManager SecretManager\n   574→}\n   575→\n   576→func (s *secretManagerOption) applyToHTTPClientOptions(opts *httpClientOptions) {\n   577→\topts.secretManager = s.secretManager\n   578→}\n   579→\n   580→func (s *secretManagerOption) applyToTLSConfigOptions(opts *tlsConfigOptions) {\n   581→\topts.secretManager = s.secretManager\n   582→}\n   583→\n   584→// SecretManagerOption is an option for providing a SecretManager.\n   585→type SecretManagerOption interface {\n   586→\tTLSConfigOption\n   587→\tHTTPClientOption\n   588→}\n   589→\n   590→// WithSecretManager allows setting the secret manager.\n   591→func WithSecretManager(manager SecretManager) SecretManagerOption {\n   592→\treturn &secretManagerOption{\n   593→\t\tsecretManager: manager,\n   594→\t}\n   595→}\n   596→\n   597→// NewClient returns a http.Client using the specified http.RoundTripper.\n   598→func newClient(rt http.RoundTripper) *http.Client {\n   599→\treturn &http.Client{Transport: rt}\n   600→}\n   601→\n   602→// NewClientFromConfig returns a new HTTP client configured for the\n   603→// given config.HTTPClientConfig and config.HTTPClientOption.\n   604→// The name is used as go-conntrack metric label.\n   605→func NewClientFromConfig(cfg HTTPClientConfig, name string, optFuncs ...HTTPClientOption) (*http.Client, error) {\n   606→\trt, err := NewRoundTripperFromConfig(cfg, name, optFuncs...)\n   607→\tif err != nil {\n   608→\t\treturn nil, err\n   609→\t}\n   610→\tclient := newClient(rt)\n   611→\tif !cfg.FollowRedirects {\n   612→\t\tclient.CheckRedirect = func(*http.Request, []*http.Request) error {\n   613→\t\t\treturn http.ErrUseLastResponse\n   614→\t\t}\n   615→\t}\n   616→\treturn client, nil\n   617→}\n   618→\n   619→// NewRoundTripperFromConfig returns a new HTTP RoundTripper configured for the\n   620→// given config.HTTPClientConfig and config.HTTPClientOption.\n   621→// The name is used as go-conntrack metric label.\n   622→func NewRoundTripperFromConfig(cfg HTTPClientConfig, name string, optFuncs ...HTTPClientOption) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n   623→\treturn NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext(context.Background(), cfg, name, optFuncs...)\n   624→}\n   625→\n   626→// NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext returns a new HTTP RoundTripper configured for the\n   627→// given config.HTTPClientConfig and config.HTTPClientOption.\n   628→// The name is used as go-conntrack metric label.\n   629→func NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext(ctx context.Context, cfg HTTPClientConfig, name string, optFuncs ...HTTPClientOption) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n   630→\topts := defaultHTTPClientOptions\n   631→\tfor _, opt := range optFuncs {\n   632→\t\topt.applyToHTTPClientOptions(&opts)\n   633→\t}\n   634→\n   635→\tvar dialContext func(ctx context.Context, network, addr string) (net.Conn, error)\n   636→\n   637→\tif opts.dialContextFunc != nil {\n   638→\t\tdialContext = conntrack.NewDialContextFunc(\n   639→\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithDialContextFunc((func(context.Context, string, string) (net.Conn, error))(opts.dialContextFunc)),\n   640→\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithTracing(),\n   641→\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithName(name))\n   642→\t} else {\n   643→\t\tdialContext = conntrack.NewDialContextFunc(\n   644→\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithTracing(),\n   645→\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithName(name))\n   646→\t}\n   647→\n   648→\tnewRT := func(tlsConfig *tls.Config) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n   649→\t\t// The only timeout we care about is the configured scrape timeout.\n   650→\t\t// It is applied on request. So we leave out any timings here.\n   651→\t\tvar rt http.RoundTripper = &http.Transport{\n   652→\t\t\tProxy:                 cfg.Proxy(),\n   653→\t\t\tProxyConnectHeader:    cfg.GetProxyConnectHeader(),\n   654→\t\t\tMaxIdleConns:          20000,\n   655→\t\t\tMaxIdleConnsPerHost:   1000, // see https://github.com/golang/go/issues/13801\n   656→\t\t\tDisableKeepAlives:     !opts.keepAlivesEnabled,\n   657→\t\t\tTLSClientConfig:       tlsConfig,\n   658→\t\t\tDisableCompression:    true,\n   659→\t\t\tIdleConnTimeout:       opts.idleConnTimeout,\n   660→\t\t\tTLSHandshakeTimeout:   10 * time.Second,\n   661→\t\t\tExpectContinueTimeout: 1 * time.Second,\n   662→\t\t\tDialContext:           dialContext,\n   663→\t\t}\n   664→\t\tif opts.http2Enabled && cfg.EnableHTTP2 {\n   665→\t\t\thttp2t, err := http2.ConfigureTransports(rt.(*http.Transport))\n   666→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   667→\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   668→\t\t\t}\n   669→\t\t\thttp2t.ReadIdleTimeout = time.Minute\n   670→\t\t}\n   671→\n   672→\t\t// If a authorization_credentials is provided, create a round tripper that will set the\n   673→\t\t// Authorization header correctly on each request.\n   674→\t\tif cfg.Authorization != nil {\n   675→\t\t\tcredentialsSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.Authorization.Credentials, cfg.Authorization.CredentialsFile, cfg.Authorization.CredentialsRef)\n   676→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   677→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use credentials: %w\", err)\n   678→\t\t\t}\n   679→\t\t\trt = NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper(cfg.Authorization.Type, credentialsSecret, rt)\n   680→\t\t}\n   681→\t\t// Backwards compatibility, be nice with importers who would not have\n   682→\t\t// called Validate().\n   683→\t\tif len(cfg.BearerToken) > 0 || len(cfg.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n   684→\t\t\tbearerSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.BearerToken, cfg.BearerTokenFile, \"\")\n   685→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   686→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use bearer token: %w\", err)\n   687→\t\t\t}\n   688→\t\t\trt = NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper(\"Bearer\", bearerSecret, rt)\n   689→\t\t}\n   690→\n   691→\t\tif cfg.BasicAuth != nil {\n   692→\t\t\tusernameSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, Secret(cfg.BasicAuth.Username), cfg.BasicAuth.UsernameFile, cfg.BasicAuth.UsernameRef)\n   693→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   694→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use username: %w\", err)\n   695→\t\t\t}\n   696→\t\t\tpasswordSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.BasicAuth.Password, cfg.BasicAuth.PasswordFile, cfg.BasicAuth.PasswordRef)\n   697→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   698→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use password: %w\", err)\n   699→\t\t\t}\n   700→\t\t\trt = NewBasicAuthRoundTripper(usernameSecret, passwordSecret, rt)\n   701→\t\t}\n   702→\n   703→\t\tif cfg.OAuth2 != nil {\n   704→\t\t\tvar (\n   705→\t\t\t\toauthCredential SecretReader\n   706→\t\t\t\terr             error\n   707→\t\t\t)\n   708→\n   709→\t\t\tif cfg.OAuth2.GrantType == grantTypeJWTBearer {\n   710→\t\t\t\toauthCredential, err = toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKey, cfg.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyFile, cfg.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyRef)\n   711→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   712→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use client certificate: %w\", err)\n   713→\t\t\t\t}\n   714→\t\t\t} else {\n   715→\t\t\t\toauthCredential, err = toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.OAuth2.ClientSecret, cfg.OAuth2.ClientSecretFile, cfg.OAuth2.ClientSecretRef)\n   716→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   717→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use client secret: %w\", err)\n   718→\t\t\t\t}\n   719→\t\t\t}\n   720→\t\t\trt = NewOAuth2RoundTripper(oauthCredential, cfg.OAuth2, rt, &opts)\n   721→\t\t}\n   722→\n   723→\t\tif cfg.HTTPHeaders != nil {\n   724→\t\t\trt = NewHeadersRoundTripper(cfg.HTTPHeaders, rt)\n   725→\t\t}\n   726→\n   727→\t\tif opts.userAgent != \"\" {\n   728→\t\t\trt = NewUserAgentRoundTripper(opts.userAgent, rt)\n   729→\t\t}\n   730→\n   731→\t\tif opts.host != \"\" {\n   732→\t\t\trt = NewHostRoundTripper(opts.host, rt)\n   733→\t\t}\n   734→\n   735→\t\t// Return a new configured RoundTripper.\n   736→\t\treturn rt, nil\n   737→\t}\n   738→\n   739→\ttlsConfig, err := opts.newTLSConfigFunc(ctx, &cfg.TLSConfig, WithSecretManager(opts.secretManager))\n   740→\tif err != nil {\n   741→\t\treturn nil, err\n   742→\t}\n   743→\n   744→\ttlsSettings, err := cfg.TLSConfig.roundTripperSettings(opts.secretManager)\n   745→\tif err != nil {\n   746→\t\treturn nil, err\n   747→\t}\n   748→\n   749→\tif tlsSettings.immutable() {\n   750→\t\t// No need for a RoundTripper that reloads the files automatically.\n   751→\t\treturn newRT(tlsConfig)\n   752→\t}\n   753→\treturn NewTLSRoundTripperWithContext(ctx, tlsConfig, tlsSettings, newRT)\n   754→}\n   755→\n   756→// SecretManager manages secret data mapped to names known as \"references\" or \"refs\".\n   757→type SecretManager interface {\n   758→\t// Fetch returns the secret data given a secret name indicated by `secretRef`.\n   759→\tFetch(ctx context.Context, secretRef string) (string, error)\n   760→}\n   761→\n   762→type SecretReader interface {\n   763→\tFetch(ctx context.Context) (string, error)\n   764→\tDescription() string\n   765→\tImmutable() bool\n   766→}\n   767→\n   768→type InlineSecret struct {\n   769→\ttext string\n   770→}\n   771→\n   772→func NewInlineSecret(text string) *InlineSecret {\n   773→\treturn &InlineSecret{text: text}\n   774→}\n   775→\n   776→func (s *InlineSecret) Fetch(context.Context) (string, error) {\n   777→\treturn s.text, nil\n   778→}\n   779→\n   780→func (*InlineSecret) Description() string {\n   781→\treturn \"inline\"\n   782→}\n   783→\n   784→func (*InlineSecret) Immutable() bool {\n   785→\treturn true\n   786→}\n   787→\n   788→type FileSecret struct {\n   789→\tfile string\n   790→}\n   791→\n   792→func NewFileSecret(file string) *FileSecret {\n   793→\treturn &FileSecret{file: file}\n   794→}\n   795→\n   796→func (s *FileSecret) Fetch(context.Context) (string, error) {\n   797→\tfileBytes, err := os.ReadFile(s.file)\n   798→\tif err != nil {\n   799→\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read file %s: %w\", s.file, err)\n   800→\t}\n   801→\treturn strings.TrimSpace(string(fileBytes)), nil\n   802→}\n   803→\n   804→func (s *FileSecret) Description() string {\n   805→\treturn \"file \" + s.file\n   806→}\n   807→\n   808→func (*FileSecret) Immutable() bool {\n   809→\treturn false\n   810→}\n   811→\n   812→// refSecret fetches a single secret from a SecretManager.\n   813→type refSecret struct {\n   814→\tref     string\n   815→\tmanager SecretManager // manager is expected to be not nil.\n   816→}\n   817→\n   818→func (s *refSecret) Fetch(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {\n   819→\treturn s.manager.Fetch(ctx, s.ref)\n   820→}\n   821→\n   822→func (s *refSecret) Description() string {\n   823→\treturn \"ref \" + s.ref\n   824→}\n   825→\n   826→func (*refSecret) Immutable() bool {\n   827→\treturn false\n   828→}\n   829→\n   830→// toSecret returns a SecretReader from one of the given sources, assuming exactly\n   831→// one or none of the sources are provided.\n   832→func toSecret(secretManager SecretManager, text Secret, file, ref string) (SecretReader, error) {\n   833→\tif text != \"\" {\n   834→\t\treturn NewInlineSecret(string(text)), nil\n   835→\t}\n   836→\tif file != \"\" {\n   837→\t\treturn NewFileSecret(file), nil\n   838→\t}\n   839→\tif ref != \"\" {\n   840→\t\tif secretManager == nil {\n   841→\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"cannot use secret ref without manager\")\n   842→\t\t}\n   843→\t\treturn &refSecret{\n   844→\t\t\tref:     ref,\n   845→\t\t\tmanager: secretManager,\n   846→\t\t}, nil\n   847→\t}\n   848→\treturn nil, nil\n   849→}\n   850→\n   851→type authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper struct {\n   852→\tauthType        string\n   853→\tauthCredentials SecretReader\n   854→\trt              http.RoundTripper\n   855→}\n   856→\n   857→// NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper adds the authorization credentials\n   858→// read from the provided SecretReader to a request unless the authorization header\n   859→// has already been set.\n   860→func NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper(authType string, authCredentials SecretReader, rt http.RoundTripper) http.RoundTripper {\n   861→\treturn &authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper{authType, authCredentials, rt}\n   862→}\n   863→\n   864→func (rt *authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n   865→\tif len(req.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")) != 0 {\n   866→\t\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n   867→\t}\n   868→\n   869→\tvar authCredentials string\n   870→\tif rt.authCredentials != nil {\n   871→\t\tvar err error\n   872→\t\tauthCredentials, err = rt.authCredentials.Fetch(req.Context())\n   873→\t\tif err != nil {\n   874→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read authorization credentials: %w\", err)\n   875→\t\t}\n   876→\t}\n   877→\n   878→\treq = cloneRequest(req)\n   879→\treq.Header.Set(\"Authorization\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %s\", rt.authType, authCredentials))\n   880→\n   881→\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n   882→}\n   883→\n   884→func (rt *authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n   885→\tif ci, ok := rt.rt.(closeIdler); ok {\n   886→\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n   887→\t}\n   888→}\n   889→\n   890→type basicAuthRoundTripper struct {\n   891→\tusername SecretReader\n   892→\tpassword SecretReader\n   893→\trt       http.RoundTripper\n   894→}\n   895→\n   896→// NewBasicAuthRoundTripper will apply a BASIC auth authorization header to a request unless it has\n   897→// already been set.\n   898→func NewBasicAuthRoundTripper(username, password SecretReader, rt http.RoundTripper) http.RoundTripper {\n   899→\treturn &basicAuthRoundTripper{username, password, rt}\n   900→}\n   901→\n   902→func (rt *basicAuthRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n   903→\tif len(req.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")) != 0 {\n   904→\t\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n   905→\t}\n   906→\tvar username string\n   907→\tvar password string\n   908→\tif rt.username != nil {\n   909→\t\tvar err error\n   910→\t\tusername, err = rt.username.Fetch(req.Context())\n   911→\t\tif err != nil {\n   912→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read basic auth username: %w\", err)\n   913→\t\t}\n   914→\t}\n   915→\tif rt.password != nil {\n   916→\t\tvar err error\n   917→\t\tpassword, err = rt.password.Fetch(req.Context())\n   918→\t\tif err != nil {\n   919→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read basic auth password: %w\", err)\n   920→\t\t}\n   921→\t}\n   922→\treq = cloneRequest(req)\n   923→\treq.SetBasicAuth(username, password)\n   924→\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n   925→}\n   926→\n   927→func (rt *basicAuthRoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n   928→\tif ci, ok := rt.rt.(closeIdler); ok {\n   929→\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n   930→\t}\n   931→}\n   932→\n   933→type oauth2RoundTripper struct {\n   934→\tmtx        sync.RWMutex\n   935→\tlastRT     *oauth2.Transport\n   936→\tlastSecret string\n   937→\n   938→\t// Required for interaction with Oauth2 server.\n   939→\tconfig          *OAuth2\n   940→\toauthCredential SecretReader\n   941→\topts            *httpClientOptions\n   942→\tclient          *http.Client\n   943→}\n   944→\n   945→func NewOAuth2RoundTripper(oauthCredential SecretReader, config *OAuth2, next http.RoundTripper, opts *httpClientOptions) http.RoundTripper {\n   946→\tif oauthCredential == nil {\n   947→\t\toauthCredential = NewInlineSecret(\"\")\n   948→\t}\n   949→\n   950→\treturn &oauth2RoundTripper{\n   951→\t\tconfig: config,\n   952→\t\t// A correct tokenSource will be added later on.\n   953→\t\tlastRT:          &oauth2.Transport{Base: next},\n   954→\t\topts:            opts,\n   955→\t\toauthCredential: oauthCredential,\n   956→\t}\n   957→}\n   958→\n   959→type oauth2TokenSourceConfig interface {\n   960→\tTokenSource(ctx context.Context) oauth2.TokenSource\n   961→}\n   962→\n   963→func (rt *oauth2RoundTripper) newOauth2TokenSource(req *http.Request, clientCredential string) (client *http.Client, source oauth2.TokenSource, err error) {\n   964→\ttlsConfig, err := NewTLSConfig(&rt.config.TLSConfig, WithSecretManager(rt.opts.secretManager))\n   965→\tif err != nil {\n   966→\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   967→\t}\n   968→\n   969→\ttlsTransport := func(tlsConfig *tls.Config) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n   970→\t\treturn &http.Transport{\n   971→\t\t\tTLSClientConfig:       tlsConfig,\n   972→\t\t\tProxy:                 rt.config.Proxy(),\n   973→\t\t\tProxyConnectHeader:    rt.config.GetProxyConnectHeader(),\n   974→\t\t\tDisableKeepAlives:     !rt.opts.keepAlivesEnabled,\n   975→\t\t\tMaxIdleConns:          20,\n   976→\t\t\tMaxIdleConnsPerHost:   1, // see https://github.com/golang/go/issues/13801\n   977→\t\t\tIdleConnTimeout:       10 * time.Second,\n   978→\t\t\tTLSHandshakeTimeout:   10 * time.Second,\n   979→\t\t\tExpectContinueTimeout: 1 * time.Second,\n   980→\t\t}, nil\n   981→\t}\n   982→\n   983→\tvar t http.RoundTripper\n   984→\ttlsSettings, err := rt.config.TLSConfig.roundTripperSettings(rt.opts.secretManager)\n   985→\tif err != nil {\n   986→\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   987→\t}\n   988→\tif tlsSettings.immutable() {\n   989→\t\tt, _ = tlsTransport(tlsConfig)\n   990→\t} else {\n   991→\t\tt, err = NewTLSRoundTripperWithContext(req.Context(), tlsConfig, tlsSettings, tlsTransport)\n   992→\t\tif err != nil {\n   993→\t\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   994→\t\t}\n   995→\t}\n   996→\n   997→\tif ua := req.UserAgent(); ua != \"\" {\n   998→\t\tt = NewUserAgentRoundTripper(ua, t)\n   999→\t}\n  1000→\n  1001→\tvar config oauth2TokenSourceConfig\n  1002→\n  1003→\tif rt.config.GrantType == grantTypeJWTBearer {\n  1004→\t\t// RFC 7523 3.1 - JWT authorization grants\n  1005→\t\t// RFC 7523 3.2 - Client Authentication Processing is not implement upstream yet,\n  1006→\t\t// see https://github.com/golang/oauth2/pull/745\n  1007→\n  1008→\t\tvar sig *jwt.SigningMethodRSA\n  1009→\t\tswitch rt.config.SignatureAlgorithm {\n  1010→\t\tcase jwt.SigningMethodRS256.Name:\n  1011→\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS256\n  1012→\t\tcase jwt.SigningMethodRS384.Name:\n  1013→\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS384\n  1014→\t\tcase jwt.SigningMethodRS512.Name:\n  1015→\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS512\n  1016→\t\tdefault:\n  1017→\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS256\n  1018→\t\t}\n  1019→\n  1020→\t\tiss := rt.config.Iss\n  1021→\t\tif iss == \"\" {\n  1022→\t\t\tiss = rt.config.ClientID\n  1023→\t\t}\n  1024→\t\tconfig = &JwtGrantTypeConfig{\n  1025→\t\t\tPrivateKey:       []byte(clientCredential),\n  1026→\t\t\tPrivateKeyID:     rt.config.ClientCertificateKeyID,\n  1027→\t\t\tScopes:           rt.config.Scopes,\n  1028→\t\t\tTokenURL:         rt.config.TokenURL,\n  1029→\t\t\tSigningAlgorithm: sig,\n  1030→\t\t\tIss:              iss,\n  1031→\t\t\tSubject:          rt.config.ClientID,\n  1032→\t\t\tAudience:         rt.config.Audience,\n  1033→\t\t\tPrivateClaims:    rt.config.Claims,\n  1034→\t\t\tEndpointParams:   mapToValues(rt.config.EndpointParams),\n  1035→\t\t}\n  1036→\t} else {\n  1037→\t\tconfig = &clientcredentials.Config{\n  1038→\t\t\tClientID:       rt.config.ClientID,\n  1039→\t\t\tClientSecret:   clientCredential,\n  1040→\t\t\tScopes:         rt.config.Scopes,\n  1041→\t\t\tTokenURL:       rt.config.TokenURL,\n  1042→\t\t\tEndpointParams: mapToValues(rt.config.EndpointParams),\n  1043→\t\t}\n  1044→\t}\n  1045→\tclient = &http.Client{Transport: t}\n  1046→\tctx := context.WithValue(context.Background(), oauth2.HTTPClient, client)\n  1047→\treturn client, config.TokenSource(ctx), nil\n  1048→}\n  1049→\n  1050→func (rt *oauth2RoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n  1051→\tvar (\n  1052→\t\tsecret    string\n  1053→\t\tneedsInit bool\n  1054→\t)\n  1055→\n  1056→\trt.mtx.RLock()\n  1057→\tsecret = rt.lastSecret\n  1058→\tneedsInit = rt.lastRT.Source == nil\n  1059→\trt.mtx.RUnlock()\n  1060→\n  1061→\t// Fetch the secret if it's our first run or always if the secret can change.\n  1062→\tif !rt.oauthCredential.Immutable() || needsInit {\n  1063→\t\tnewSecret, err := rt.oauthCredential.Fetch(req.Context())\n  1064→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1065→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read oauth2 client secret: %w\", err)\n  1066→\t\t}\n  1067→\t\tif newSecret != secret || needsInit {\n  1068→\t\t\t// Secret changed or it's a first run. Rebuilt oauth2 setup.\n  1069→\t\t\tclient, source, err := rt.newOauth2TokenSource(req, newSecret)\n  1070→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n  1071→\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n  1072→\t\t\t}\n  1073→\n  1074→\t\t\trt.mtx.Lock()\n  1075→\t\t\trt.lastSecret = newSecret\n  1076→\t\t\trt.lastRT.Source = source\n  1077→\t\t\tif rt.client != nil {\n  1078→\t\t\t\trt.client.CloseIdleConnections()\n  1079→\t\t\t}\n  1080→\t\t\trt.client = client\n  1081→\t\t\trt.mtx.Unlock()\n  1082→\t\t}\n  1083→\t}\n  1084→\n  1085→\trt.mtx.RLock()\n  1086→\tcurrentRT := rt.lastRT\n  1087→\trt.mtx.RUnlock()\n  1088→\treturn currentRT.RoundTrip(req)\n  1089→}\n  1090→\n  1091→func (rt *oauth2RoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n  1092→\tif rt.client != nil {\n  1093→\t\trt.client.CloseIdleConnections()\n  1094→\t}\n  1095→\tif ci, ok := rt.lastRT.Base.(closeIdler); ok {\n  1096→\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n  1097→\t}\n  1098→}\n  1099→\n  1100→func mapToValues(m map[string]string) url.Values {\n  1101→\tv := url.Values{}\n  1102→\tfor name, value := range m {\n  1103→\t\tv.Set(name, value)\n  1104→\t}\n  1105→\n  1106→\treturn v\n  1107→}\n  1108→\n  1109→// cloneRequest returns a clone of the provided *http.Request.\n  1110→// The clone is a shallow copy of the struct and its Header map.\n  1111→func cloneRequest(r *http.Request) *http.Request {\n  1112→\t// Shallow copy of the struct.\n  1113→\tr2 := new(http.Request)\n  1114→\t*r2 = *r\n  1115→\t// Deep copy of the Header.\n  1116→\tr2.Header = make(http.Header)\n  1117→\tfor k, s := range r.Header {\n  1118→\t\tr2.Header[k] = s\n  1119→\t}\n  1120→\treturn r2\n  1121→}\n  1122→\n  1123→type tlsConfigOptions struct {\n  1124→\tsecretManager SecretManager\n  1125→}\n  1126→\n  1127→// TLSConfigOption defines an option that can be applied to the HTTP client.\n  1128→type TLSConfigOption interface {\n  1129→\tapplyToTLSConfigOptions(options *tlsConfigOptions)\n  1130→}\n  1131→\n  1132→// NewTLSConfig creates a new tls.Config from the given TLSConfig.\n  1133→func NewTLSConfig(cfg *TLSConfig, optFuncs ...TLSConfigOption) (*tls.Config, error) {\n  1134→\treturn NewTLSConfigWithContext(context.Background(), cfg, optFuncs...)\n  1135→}\n  1136→\n  1137→// NewTLSConfigWithContext creates a new tls.Config from the given TLSConfig.\n  1138→func NewTLSConfigWithContext(ctx context.Context, cfg *TLSConfig, optFuncs ...TLSConfigOption) (*tls.Config, error) {\n  1139→\topts := tlsConfigOptions{}\n  1140→\tfor _, opt := range optFuncs {\n  1141→\t\topt.applyToTLSConfigOptions(&opts)\n  1142→\t}\n  1143→\n  1144→\tif err := cfg.Validate(); err != nil {\n  1145→\t\treturn nil, err\n  1146→\t}\n  1147→\n  1148→\ttlsConfig := &tls.Config{\n  1149→\t\tInsecureSkipVerify: cfg.InsecureSkipVerify,\n  1150→\t\tMinVersion:         uint16(cfg.MinVersion),\n  1151→\t\tMaxVersion:         uint16(cfg.MaxVersion),\n  1152→\t}\n  1153→\n  1154→\tif cfg.MaxVersion != 0 && cfg.MinVersion != 0 {\n  1155→\t\tif cfg.MaxVersion < cfg.MinVersion {\n  1156→\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"tls_config.max_version must be greater than or equal to tls_config.min_version if both are specified\")\n  1157→\t\t}\n  1158→\t}\n  1159→\n  1160→\t// If a CA cert is provided then let's read it in so we can validate the\n  1161→\t// scrape target's certificate properly.\n  1162→\tcaSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, Secret(cfg.CA), cfg.CAFile, cfg.CARef)\n  1163→\tif err != nil {\n  1164→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use CA cert: %w\", err)\n  1165→\t}\n  1166→\tif caSecret != nil {\n  1167→\t\tca, err := caSecret.Fetch(ctx)\n  1168→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1169→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read CA cert: %w\", err)\n  1170→\t\t}\n  1171→\t\tif !updateRootCA(tlsConfig, []byte(ca)) {\n  1172→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use specified CA cert %s\", caSecret.Description())\n  1173→\t\t}\n  1174→\t}\n  1175→\n  1176→\tif len(cfg.ServerName) > 0 {\n  1177→\t\ttlsConfig.ServerName = cfg.ServerName\n  1178→\t}\n  1179→\n  1180→\t// If a client cert & key is provided then configure TLS config accordingly.\n  1181→\tif cfg.usingClientCert() && cfg.usingClientKey() {\n  1182→\t\t// Verify that client cert and key are valid.\n  1183→\t\tif _, err := cfg.getClientCertificate(ctx, opts.secretManager); err != nil {\n  1184→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n  1185→\t\t}\n  1186→\t\ttlsConfig.GetClientCertificate = func(cri *tls.CertificateRequestInfo) (*tls.Certificate, error) {\n  1187→\t\t\tvar ctx context.Context\n  1188→\t\t\tif cri != nil {\n  1189→\t\t\t\tctx = cri.Context()\n  1190→\t\t\t}\n  1191→\t\t\treturn cfg.getClientCertificate(ctx, opts.secretManager)\n  1192→\t\t}\n  1193→\t}\n  1194→\n  1195→\treturn tlsConfig, nil\n  1196→}\n  1197→\n  1198→// TLSConfig configures the options for TLS connections.\n  1199→type TLSConfig struct {\n  1200→\t// Text of the CA cert to use for the targets.\n  1201→\tCA string `yaml:\"ca,omitempty\" json:\"ca,omitempty\"`\n  1202→\t// Text of the client cert file for the targets.\n  1203→\tCert string `yaml:\"cert,omitempty\" json:\"cert,omitempty\"`\n  1204→\t// Text of the client key file for the targets.\n  1205→\tKey Secret `yaml:\"key,omitempty\" json:\"key,omitempty\"`\n  1206→\t// The CA cert to use for the targets.\n  1207→\tCAFile string `yaml:\"ca_file,omitempty\" json:\"ca_file,omitempty\"`\n  1208→\t// The client cert file for the targets.\n  1209→\tCertFile string `yaml:\"cert_file,omitempty\" json:\"cert_file,omitempty\"`\n  1210→\t// The client key file for the targets.\n  1211→\tKeyFile string `yaml:\"key_file,omitempty\" json:\"key_file,omitempty\"`\n  1212→\t// CARef is the name of the secret within the secret manager to use as the CA cert for the\n  1213→\t// targets.\n  1214→\tCARef string `yaml:\"ca_ref,omitempty\" json:\"ca_ref,omitempty\"`\n  1215→\t// CertRef is the name of the secret within the secret manager to use as the client cert for\n  1216→\t// the targets.\n  1217→\tCertRef string `yaml:\"cert_ref,omitempty\" json:\"cert_ref,omitempty\"`\n  1218→\t// KeyRef is the name of the secret within the secret manager to use as the client key for\n  1219→\t// the targets.\n  1220→\tKeyRef string `yaml:\"key_ref,omitempty\" json:\"key_ref,omitempty\"`\n  1221→\t// Used to verify the hostname for the targets.\n  1222→\tServerName string `yaml:\"server_name,omitempty\" json:\"server_name,omitempty\"`\n  1223→\t// Disable target certificate validation.\n  1224→\tInsecureSkipVerify bool `yaml:\"insecure_skip_verify\" json:\"insecure_skip_verify\"`\n  1225→\t// Minimum TLS version.\n  1226→\tMinVersion TLSVersion `yaml:\"min_version,omitempty\" json:\"min_version,omitempty\"`\n  1227→\t// Maximum TLS version.\n  1228→\tMaxVersion TLSVersion `yaml:\"max_version,omitempty\" json:\"max_version,omitempty\"`\n  1229→}\n  1230→\n  1231→// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\n  1232→func (c *TLSConfig) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n  1233→\tif c == nil {\n  1234→\t\treturn\n  1235→\t}\n  1236→\tc.CAFile = JoinDir(dir, c.CAFile)\n  1237→\tc.CertFile = JoinDir(dir, c.CertFile)\n  1238→\tc.KeyFile = JoinDir(dir, c.KeyFile)\n  1239→}\n  1240→\n  1241→// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\n  1242→func (c *TLSConfig) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(interface{}) error) error {\n  1243→\ttype plain TLSConfig\n  1244→\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(c)); err != nil {\n  1245→\t\treturn err\n  1246→\t}\n  1247→\treturn c.Validate()\n  1248→}\n  1249→\n  1250→// Validate validates the TLSConfig to check that only one of the inlined or\n  1251→// file-based fields for the TLS CA, client
